import { SchedulingRunsModule } from './modules/scheduling-runs/scheduling-runs.module';
import { SchoolClosuresModule } from './modules/school-closures/school-closures.module';
import { SearchModule } from './modules/search/search.module';
import { SecurityIncidentsModule } from './modules/security-incidents/security-incidents.module';
import { SenModule } from './modules/sen/sen.module';
import { StaffAvailabilityModule } from './modules/staff-availability/staff-availability.module';
import { StaffPreferencesModule } from './modules/staff-preferences/staff-preferences.module';
import { StaffProfilesModule } from './modules/staff-profiles/staff-profiles.module';
import { StaffWellbeingModule } from './modules/staff-wellbeing/staff-wellbeing.module';
import { StudentsModule } from './modules/students/students.module';
import { TenantsModule } from './modules/tenants/tenants.module';
import { WebsiteModule } from './modules/website/website.module';

@Module({
  providers: [
    {
      provide: APP_FILTER,
      useClass: SentryGlobalFilter,
    },
    {
      provide: APP_GUARD,
      useClass: ThrottlerGuard,
    },
  ],
  imports: [
    SentryModule.forRoot(),
    ThrottlerModule.forRoot([{ ttl: 60000, limit: 100 }]),
    ConfigModule,
    BullModule.forRootAsync({
      useFactory: (configService: ConfigService) => {
        const url = new URL(configService.get<string>('REDIS_URL')!);
        return {
          connection: {
            host: url.hostname,
            port: parseInt(url.port, 10) || 6379,
            password: url.password ? decodeURIComponent(url.password) : undefined,
          },
        };
      },
      inject: [ConfigService],
    }),
    BullModule.registerQueue({ name: 'pastoral' }),
    PrismaModule,
    RedisModule,
    CommonModule,
    HealthModule,
    AuthModule,
    S3Module,
    TenantsModule,
    ConfigurationModule,
    PreferencesModule,
    RbacModule,
    ApprovalsModule,
    AdmissionsModule,
    StaffProfilesModule,
    AcademicsModule,
    StudentsModule,
    ClassesModule,
    ChildProtectionModule,
    RoomsModule,
    SchedulesModule,
    RegulatoryModule,
    SchoolClosuresModule,
    AttendanceModule,
    BehaviourModule,
    CriticalIncidentsModule,
    HomeworkModule,
    HouseholdsModule,
    ParentsModule,
    PastoralModule,
    PastoralCheckinsModule,
    PastoralDsarModule,
    SearchModule,
    DashboardModule,
    EarlyWarningModule,
    EngagementModule,
    PeriodGridModule,
    ClassRequirementsModule,
    StaffAvailabilityModule,
    StaffPreferencesModule,
    SchedulingRunsModule,
    GradebookModule,
    PdfRenderingModule,
    FinanceModule,
    GdprModule,
    PayrollModule,
    CommunicationsModule,
    ParentInquiriesModule,
    WebsiteModule,
    AuditLogModule,
    ComplianceModule,
    ImportsModule,
    ReportsModule,
    RegistrationModule,
    SchedulingModule,
    StaffWellbeingModule,
    SecurityIncidentsModule,
    SenModule,
  ],
})
export class AppModule implements NestModule {
  configure(consumer: MiddlewareConsumer) {
    // Correlation middleware runs first — assigns X-Request-Id before any other middleware
    consumer.apply(CorrelationMiddleware, RequestLoggingMiddleware).forRoutes('*');

    consumer
      .apply(TenantResolutionMiddleware)
      .exclude(
        { path: 'health', method: RequestMethod.ALL },
        { path: 'health/(.*)', method: RequestMethod.ALL },
        { path: 'docs(.*)', method: RequestMethod.ALL },
        { path: 'v1/stripe/webhook', method: RequestMethod.POST },
        { path: 'v1/webhooks/(.*)', method: RequestMethod.POST },
      )
      .forRoutes('*');
  }
}

===== CI workflow =====
$ sh -lc cat .github/workflows/ci.yml 2>/dev/null
name: CI / Deploy

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  ci:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    env:
      SENTRY_ENVIRONMENT: ci
      SENTRY_RELEASE: ${{ github.sha }}
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:16
        env:
          POSTGRES_USER: prisma
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: password
          POSTGRES_DB: edupod_test
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
      redis:
        image: redis:7
        ports:
          - 6379:6379
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v5
        with:
          fetch-depth: 0

      - name: Secret scanning
        uses: gitleaks/gitleaks-action@v2
        env:
          GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}

      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v5

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v5
        with:
          node-version: '24'
          cache: 'pnpm'
          package-manager-cache: false

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: Security audit
        run: pnpm audit --audit-level=high
        continue-on-error: true  # Warn on known transitive vulns (xlsx, glob, next, tar) — tracked for upgrade

      - name: Generate Prisma client
        run: pnpm --filter @school/prisma exec prisma generate

      - name: Verify worker processor specs
        run: pnpm check:worker-processor-specs

      - name: Check i18n completeness
        run: pnpm i18n:check

      - name: Check hotspot complexity budgets
        run: pnpm hotspots:check

      - name: Lint
        run: pnpm turbo run lint

      - name: Type check
        run: pnpm turbo run type-check
        env:
          NODE_OPTIONS: '--max-old-space-size=8192'

      - name: Module cohesion check
        run: node scripts/check-module-cohesion.js
        continue-on-error: true

      - name: Module tier dependency check
        run: node scripts/check-module-tiers.js

      - name: Global provider registry check
        run: node scripts/check-global-providers.js

      - name: Cross-module dependency check
        run: node scripts/check-cross-module-deps.js
        continue-on-error: true

      - name: Run unit tests with coverage enforcement
        run: pnpm --filter @school/api --filter @school/worker run test:coverage && pnpm --filter @school/shared --filter @school/web --filter @school/prisma run test

      - name: Test coverage gate
        run: pnpm run check:test-gate

      - name: Setup Test Database
        run: |
          psql "postgresql://prisma:password@localhost:5432/edupod_test" -c "DO \$\$ BEGIN CREATE TYPE timerange AS RANGE (subtype = time); EXCEPTION WHEN duplicate_object THEN null; END \$\$;"
          pnpm --filter @school/prisma exec prisma migrate deploy
          pnpm db:post-migrate
          pnpm db:seed
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql://prisma:password@localhost:5432/edupod_test?schema=public
          REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:6379

      - name: Run integration and e2e tests
        run: pnpm --filter @school/api run test:integration
        env:
          API_PORT: '0'
          APP_URL: http://localhost:3000
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql://prisma:password@localhost:5432/edupod_test?schema=public
          ENCRYPTION_KEY: aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa
          JWT_REFRESH_SECRET: 1a5be597a11a3d357ec51c55b88bdd4fe6a138f9f816dd0e8f048d802f87b2b3
          JWT_SECRET: 73e10ad593c9fb3e3c0aaef14332e1f4f38dfe27bb579e35ef57e8303a767d48
          MFA_ISSUER: SchoolOS-Test
          NODE_ENV: test
          PLATFORM_DOMAIN: edupod.app
          REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:6379

      - name: Build
        run: pnpm build --force

  deploy:
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    needs: [ci]
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    env:
      SENTRY_ENVIRONMENT: production
    concurrency:
      group: production-deploy
      cancel-in-progress: false
    steps:
      - name: Deploy to server
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v1.0.0
        env:
          DEPLOY_SHA: ${{ github.sha }}
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.SSH_HOST }}
          username: ${{ secrets.SSH_USER }}
          key: ${{ secrets.SSH_PRIVATE_KEY }}
          command_timeout: 20m
          envs: DEPLOY_SHA
          script: |
            cd /opt/edupod/app
            DEPLOY_SHA="$DEPLOY_SHA" SENTRY_ENVIRONMENT="$SENTRY_ENVIRONMENT" bash scripts/deploy-production.sh

  integration:
    needs: [ci]
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    timeout-minutes: 45
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:16
        env:
          POSTGRES_DB: school_platform
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: localpassword
          POSTGRES_USER: postgres
        ports:
          - 5553:5432
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "pg_isready -U postgres -d school_platform"
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
      redis:
        image: redis:7
        ports:
          - 5554:6379
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "redis-cli ping"
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
    env:
      API_PORT: '0'
      APP_URL: http://localhost:5551
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://postgres:localpassword@localhost:5553/school_platform
      ENCRYPTION_KEY: aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa
      JWT_REFRESH_SECRET: 1a5be597a11a3d357ec51c55b88bdd4fe6a138f9f816dd0e8f048d802f87b2b3
      JWT_SECRET: 73e10ad593c9fb3e3c0aaef14332e1f4f38dfe27bb579e35ef57e8303a767d48
      MFA_ISSUER: SchoolOS-Test
      NODE_ENV: test
      PLATFORM_DOMAIN: edupod.app
      REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:5554
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v5

      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v5

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v5
        with:
          node-version: '24'
          cache: 'pnpm'
          package-manager-cache: false

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: Generate Prisma client
        run: pnpm --filter @school/prisma exec prisma generate

      - name: Build shared packages
        run: pnpm --filter @school/shared --filter @school/prisma run build

      - name: Apply Prisma migrations
        run: pnpm --filter @school/prisma exec prisma migrate deploy

      - name: Apply post-migrate SQL
        run: pnpm db:post-migrate

      - name: Seed base data
        run: pnpm db:seed

      - name: Run integration tests
        run: pnpm test:integration

  visual:
    needs: [ci]
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    timeout-minutes: 30
    env:
      API_URL: http://localhost:5552
      APP_URL: http://localhost:5551
      NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL: ''
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v5

      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v5

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v5
        with:
          node-version: '24'
          cache: 'pnpm'
          package-manager-cache: false

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: Install Playwright browser
        run: pnpm --filter @school/web exec playwright install --with-deps chromium

      - name: Run visual smoke tests
        run: pnpm test:visual

      - name: Upload Playwright report
        if: failure()
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: playwright-visual-report
          path: |
            apps/web/e2e/playwright-report
            apps/web/e2e/test-results
          if-no-files-found: ignore

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16
    container_name: school-db
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - '5553:5432'
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: postgres
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: localpassword
      POSTGRES_DB: school_platform
    volumes:
      - school_pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init-db.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ['CMD-SHELL', 'pg_isready -U postgres']
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 5

  pgbouncer:
    image: edoburu/pgbouncer:1.25.1-p0
    container_name: school-pgbouncer
    restart: unless-stopped
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    ports:
      - '6432:5432'
    environment:
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://postgres:localpassword@postgres:5432/school_platform
      DEFAULT_POOL_SIZE: 20
      IGNORE_STARTUP_PARAMETERS: extra_float_digits
      MAX_CLIENT_CONN: 200
      POOL_MODE: transaction
    healthcheck:
      test: ['CMD-SHELL', 'pg_isready -h 127.0.0.1 -p 5432 -U postgres -d school_platform']
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 10

  redis:
    image: redis:7
    container_name: school-redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - '5554:6379'
    volumes:
      - school_redis:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ['CMD', 'redis-cli', 'ping']
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 5

  meilisearch:
    image: getmeili/meilisearch:latest
    container_name: school-search
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - '5555:7700'
    environment:
      MEILI_MASTER_KEY: local-dev-master-key
      MEILI_ENV: development
    volumes:
      - school_meili:/meili_data
    healthcheck:
      test: ['CMD', 'curl', '-f', 'http://localhost:7700/health']
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 5
